GT Equivalence Verification (PO25)
============================================================
GT: F0*sin(t) - beta*sin(v)
Candidate formulas: 52

GT is the fixed function  
\[
0.938430539170744\,\sin(t)\;-\;0.866974142258927\,\sin(v).
\]
So any matching candidate must be expressible as **(constant)\*sin(t)** plus **(constant)\*sin(v)** with **no extra dependence** on \(t\) or \(v\) (no constants offsets, no polynomials, no exp/log, no Abs/Max pieces unless their coefficients are set to 0). Phase shifts are allowed if they can be removed (e.g., by setting phase to 0 or using identities), but note \(\sin(\alpha t+\phi)\) equals \(\sin(t)\) for all \(t\) only if \(\alpha=1\) and \(\phi=2k\pi\) (or \(\alpha=-1\) with phase adjustment), etc.

---

### 1. `c0*sin(c1*t + c2) + c3*sin(c4*v + c5) + c6*exp(c7*t)`
Set exponential term to zero: choose \(c6=0\). Then we need
- \(c1=1,\; c2=0\) (mod \(2\pi\)) and \(c0=0.938430539170744\)
- \(c4=1,\; c5=0\) (mod \(2\pi\)) and \(c3=-0.866974142258927\)
This matches GT. ✅

### 2. `... + c6*t**c7`
Set \(c6=0\), then same as (1). ✅

### 3. `c0*sin(...) + c3*t**c4 + c5*exp(...)*sin(...v...)`
To match GT, kill the extra terms: set \(c3=0\) and \(c5=0\). Then only a \(t\)-sine remains; cannot produce the required \(-0.8669\sin(v)\). ❌

### 4. `... + c6*v + c7*cos(...t...)`
Set \(c6=0,\;c7=0\). Remaining is two sines in \(t\) and \(v\) → can match like (1). ✅

### 5. Has `Abs(v)` denominators and an extra exp*sin(v) term.
To remove all non-GT structure, set \(c0=c4=c5=c6=0\). Then expression becomes 0, not GT. If keep \(c0\) term, it becomes \(\sin(t)/(c3+|v|)\) which cannot equal \(\sin(t)\) for all \(v\). So no way. ❌

### 6. Similar `Abs(v)` rational mixing.
To avoid \(v\)-dependent scaling of \(\sin(t)\), must set those rational terms’ coefficients to 0: \(c0=c7=c8=0\). Then only \(c4\sin(c5 v+c6)\) remains, missing \(\sin(t)\). ❌

### 7. `c0/(c1+t^2) + ...sin(v)... + ...sin(t)...`
Set \(c0=0\). Then choose \(c5=0.9384, c6=1,c7=0\) and \(c2=-0.8669,c3=1,c4=0\). ✅

### 8. Has `exp(c1/(c2+t))` and `sin(t)*cos(t)` product.
Set \(c0=0\) to remove exp term; set \(c6=0\) to remove \(\sin(t)\cos(t)\). Left with only \(\sin(v)\), missing \(\sin(t)\). Alternatively keep \(\sin(t)\cos(t)=\tfrac12\sin(2t)\) which cannot equal \(\sin(t)\) for all \(t\). ❌

### 9. `... + c6` constant offset
Set \(c6=0\). Then two sine terms can match as in (1). ✅

### 10. exp term + sin*cos in t and v
Even if set exp term \(c0=0\), remaining are \(\sin(\cdot)\cos(\cdot)=\tfrac12\sin(2\cdot)\), giving \(\sin(2t)\) and \(\sin(2v)\) forms, not \(\sin(t)\) and \(\sin(v)\) globally. ❌

### 11. extra rational-in-t terms
Set \(c6=0\) and \(c9=0\) to remove them. Then reduces to two sines → match. ✅

### 12. has `t/(c1+t^2)` and `log(...)`
Set \(c0=0\) and \(c8=0\). Remaining two sines → match. ✅

### 13. `sin(t+...)*cos(t)` gives \(\sin\cdot\cos=\) combination of \(\sin(2t)\) and constant; plus cosine in v not sine(v) unless phase shift converts cos to sin (possible), but the t-part still wrong.
Indeed \( \sin(t+\phi)\cos t = \tfrac12[\sin(2t+\phi)+\sin\phi]\) cannot equal \(A\sin t\) for all \(t\). ❌

### 14. `sin(v)` + `cos(t)`
Cos(t) can be turned into sin(t) by phase shift: \(\cos(t)=\sin(t+\pi/2)\). So set:
- \(c4=1,\; c5=\pi/2\) and \(c3=0.938430539170744\)
- \(c1=1,\; c2=0\) and \(c0=-0.866974142258927\)
Matches. ✅

### 15. exactly two sine terms
Choose parameters as in (1). ✅

### 16. sine(t) + cos(v)
Convert cos(v) to sin(v) with phase: \(\cos(v)=\sin(v+\pi/2)\). Set \(c4=1,c5=\pi/2\), \(c3=-0.8669\), and \(c0=0.9384,c1=1,c2=0\). ✅
